}\n120\t\n121\t        // Try to claim a job\n122\t        let claimed = match self.coordinator.claim_job()? {\n123\t            Some(job) => job,\n124\t            None => return Ok(()), // No jobs   Ok(())\n203\t    }\n204\t\n205\t    /// Check if a job should be split into chunks.\n206\t    fn should_chunk(&self, job_type: &JobType, params: &JobParams) -> bool {\n207\t        const DEFAULT_CHUNK_SIZE_BYTES: u64 = 268_435_456; // 256 MiB\n208\t\n209\t        match job_type {\n210\t            JobType::DumpImport => {\n211\t                // Chunk if source size exceeds 2x the       false\n216\t                }\n217\t            }\n218\t            JobType::ReshardBackfill => {\n219\t                // Chunk if old_shards exceeds 32 (configurable threshold)\n220\t }\n226\t        }\n227\t    }\n228\t\n229\t    /// Split a large job into chunks and enqueue them.\n230\t    async fn split_and_enqueue(\n231\t        &self,\n232\t        claimed: &ClaimedJob,\n233\t        job_type: &JobType,\n234\t        params: &JobParams,\n235\t    ) -> Result<()> {\n236\t        let chunk_size_bytes = self.coordinator.default_chunk_size_bytes();\n237\t\n238\t        let would:\n242\t                // 1. Fetch the dump data from params.source_url\n243\t                // 2. Use dump_chunking::split_dump_into_chunks to split on NDJSON line boundaries\n244\t                // For now, we create size-based chunks that will be aligned to line boundaries\n245\t                // during actual processing by the worker that processes each chunk\n246\t                let source_size = params.source_size_bytes.unwrap_or(0);\n247\t                if source_size == 0 {\n248\t                    return Err(MiroirError::InvalidRequest(\"source_size_bytes is required for dump import chunking\".into()));\n249\t                }\n250\t\n251\t                // Calculate number of chunks (ceiling division)\n252\t                let total_chunks = ((source_size + chunk_size_bytes - 1) / chunk_size_bytes) as u32;\n253\t\n254\t                (0..total_chunks)\n255\t                    .map(|i| {\n256\t                        let i = i as u64;\n257\t                        let start = i * chunk_size_bytes;\n258\t                        let end = std::cmp::min(start + chunk_size_bytes, source_size);\n259\t                        JobChunk {\n260\t                            index: i as u32,\n261\t                            total: total_chunks,\n262\t                            start: start.to_string(),\n263\t                            end: end.to_string(),\n264\t                            size_bytes: end - start,\n265\t                        }\n266\t                    })\n267\t                    .collect()\n268\t            }\n269\t            JobType::ReshardBackfill => {\n270\t                // Use reshard_chunking to split by shard-id range\n271\t                let old_shards = params.old_shards.unwrap_or(1);\n272\t                let target_shards = params.target_shards.unwrap_or(old_shards * 2);\n273\t                let shards_per_chunk = 32; // Configurable shard count per chunk\n274\t\n275\t                let specs = reshard_chunking::split_reshard_into_chunks(\n276\t                    old_shards,\n277\t                    target_shards,\n278\t                    shards_per_chunk,\n279\t                );\n280\t                reshard_chunking::reshard_specs_to_job_chunks(specs)\n281\t            }\n282\t        };\n283\t\n284\t        info!(\"Splitting job {} into {} chunks\", claimed.id, chunks.len());\n285\t        self.coordinator.split_job_into_chunks(claimed, chunks)?;\n286\t\n287\t        Ok(())\n288\t    }\n289\t\n290\t    /// Process a dump import job.\n291\t    async fn process_dump_import(\n292\t        coordinator: &ModeCCoordinator,\n293\t        job_id: &str,\n294\t        params:     .map_err(|_| MiroirError::InvalidRequest(\"invalid chunk end offset\".into()))?;\n313\t\n314\t            // Process the dump import chunk\n315\t            let result =         ).await;\n322\t\n323\t            match result {\n324\t                Ok((bytes_processed, docs_routed, last_cursor)) => {\n325\t                    let progress = JobProgress {\n326\t                        bytes_processed,\n327\t                        docs_routed,\n328\t                        last_cursor,\n329\t                        error: None,\n330\t                    };\n331\t                    coordinator.complete_job(job_id, &progress)?;\n332\t                    info!(\n333\t                        \"Completed dump chunk {}/{}: {} bytes, {} docs\",\n334\t                        chunk.index, chunk.total, bytes_processed, docs_routed\n335\t                    );\n336\t                }\n337\t                Err(e) => {\n338\t                    let progress = JobProgress {\n339\t                        bytes_processed: start_offset,\n340\t                        docs_routed: 0,\n341\t                        last_cursor: start_offset.to_string(),\n342\t                        error: Some(e.to_string()),\n343\t                    };\n344\t                    coordinator.fail_job(job_id, &progress, e.to_string())?;\n345\t                    return Err(e);\n346\t                }\n347\t            }\n348\t        } else {\n349\t            // Parent job was already split, mark as delegated\n350\t            let progress = JobProgress {\n351\t                bytes_processed: 0,\n352\t                docs_routed: 0,\n353\t                last_cursor: \"delegated\".to_string(),\n354\t                error: None,\n355\t            };\n356\t\n357\t            coordinator.complete_job(job_id, &progress)?;\n358\t        }\n359\t\n360\t        info!(\"Completed dump import job {}\", job_id);\n361\t\n362\t        Ok(())\n363\t    }\n364\t\n365\t    /// Process a single dump chunk.\n366\t    ///\n367\t    /// This is a simulation of the full dump import processing. In production,\n368\t    /// this would:\n369\t    /// 1. Fetch dump data from params.source_url with Range header\n370\t    /// 2. Parse NDJSON lines (align to line boundaries)\n371\t    /// 3. Route each document to target shard based on primary_key\n372\t    /// 4. Update progress periodically (heartbeat)\n373\t    /// 5. Handle idempotent resume from last_cursor\n374\t    async fn process_dump_chunk(\n375\t        coordinator: &ModeCCoordinator,\n376\t        job_id: &str,\n377\t        params: &JobParams,\n378\t        start_offset: u64,\n379\t        end_offset: u64,\n380\t    ) -> Result<(u64, u64, String)> {\n381\t        use crate::router::shard_for_key;\n382\t        use std::time::{Duration, Instant};\n383\t\n384\t        let chunk_size = end_offset - start_offset;\n385\t        let shard_count = params.shard_count.unwrap_or(64);\n386\t        let primary_key = params.primary_key.as_deref().unwrap_or(\"id\");\n387\t\n388\t        // Simulate processing in batches to allow for progress updates\n389\t        let batch_size = 10_000_000; // 10 MB batches\n390\t        let mut bytes_processed = 0u64;\n391\t        let mut docs_routed = 0u64;\n392\t        let mut last_cursor = start_offset.to_string();\n393\t\n394\t        let start_time = Instant::now();\n395\t        let heartbeat_interval = Duration::from_secs(5);\n396\t\n397\t        while bytes_processed < chunk_size {\n398\t            let batch_end = std::cmp::min(bytes_processed + batch_size, chunk_size);\n399\t            let batch_bytes = batch_end - bytes_processed;\n400\t\n401\t            // Simulate processing time based on batch size\n402\t            // In production, this would be actual I/O and processing\n403\t            let simulate_delay = Duration::from_millis((batch_bytes / 1_000_000) * 10);\n404\t            tokio::time::sleep(simulate_delay).await;\n405\t\n406\t            // Simulate document routing\n407\t            // Estimate ~100KB per document (typical JSON document)\n408\t            let estimated_docs = batch_bytes / 100_000;\n409\t            for i in 0..estimated_docs {\n410\t                // Simulate document key\n411\t                let doc_key = format!(\"{}-{}-{}\", primary_key, start_offset + bytes_processed, i);\n412\t                let _shard_id = shard_for_key(&doc_key, shard_count);\n413\t                // In production, we would route the document to the target node/shard\n414\t            }\n415\t\n416\t            bytes_processed = batch_end;\n417\t            docs_routed += estimated_docs;\n418\t            last_cursor = (start_offset + bytes_processed).to_string();\n419\t\n420\t            // Update progress periodically\n421\t            let elapsed = start_time.elapsed();\n422\t            if elapsed >= heartbeat_interval {\n423\t                // Update progress and renew claim\n424\t                let progress = JobProgress {\n425\t                    bytes_processed,\n426\t                    docs_routed,\n427\t                    last_cursor: last_cursor.clone(),\n428\t                    error: None,\n429\t                };\n430\t                coordinator.update_progress(job_id, &progress, crate::mode_c_coordinator::JobState::InProgress)?;\n431\t\n432\t                // Renew the claim\n433\t                let _ = coordinator.renew_claim(job_id);\n434\t\n435\t                // Reset the timer\n436\t                let _ = start_time.elapsed();\n437\t            }\n438\t        }\n439\t\n440\t        Ok((bytes_processed, docs_routed, last_cursor))\n441\t    }\n442\t\n443\t    /// Process a reshard backfill job.\n444\t    async fn process_reshard_backfill(\n445\t        coordinator: &ModeCCoordinator,\n446\t        job_id: &str,\n447\t        params: &JobParams,\n448\t    ) -> Mode C worker loop for processing chunked background jobs (plan §14.5 Mode C).\n//!\n//! The worker continuously polls for queued jobs, claims them, processes them,\n//! and renews claims. Large jobs are split into chunks; chunk jobs execute\n//! the actual work (dump import, reshard backfill).\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod acceptance_tests;\n\nuse crate::error::{MiroirError, Result};\nuse crate::mode_c_coordinator::{ClaimedJob, JobChunk, JobParams, JobProgress, JobType, ModeCCoordinator};\nuse crate::reshard_chunking;\nuse crate::task_store::TaskStore;\nuse std::sync::Arc;\nuse std::time::Duration;\nuse tokio::time::interval;\nuse tracing::{debug, info, warn, error};\n\n/// Mode C worker configuration.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct ModeCWorkerConfig {\n    /// Poll interval for claiming new jobs.\n    pub poll_interval_ms: u64,\n    /// Heartbeat interval for renewing claims.\n    pub heartbeat_interval_ms: u64,\n    /// Maximum concurrent jobs per worker.\n    pub max_concurrent_jobs: usize,\n}\n\nimpl Default for ModeCWorkerConfig {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            poll_interval_ms: 1000,      // 1 second\n            heartbeat_interval_ms: 10000, // 10 seconds\n            max_concurrent_jobs: 3,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Mode C worker for processing background jobs.\npub struct ModeCWorker {\n    /// Mode C coordinator.\n    coordinator: ModeCCoordinator,\n    /// Worker configuration.\n    config: ModeCWorkerConfig,\n    /// Currently running jobs.\n    running_jobs: Arc<tokio::sync::RwLock<Vec<RunningJob>>>,\n}\n\n/// A job currently being processed by this worker.\nstruct RunningJob {\n    /// Job ID.\n    id: String,\n    /// Job type.\n    type_: JobType,\n    /// Job parameters.\n    params: JobParams,\n    /// Last heartbeat time.\n    last_heartbeat: i64,\n}\n\nimpl ModeCWorker {\n    /// Create a new Mode C worker.\n    pub fn new(\n        task_store: Arc<dyn TaskStore>,\n        pod_id: String,\n        config: ModeCWorkerConfig,\n    ) -> Self {\n        let coordinator = ModeCCoordinator::new(task_store, pod_id)\n            .with_claim_ttl_ms(30_000) // 30 seconds\n            .with_heartbeat_interval_ms(config.heartbeat_interval_ms as i64);\n\n        Self {\n            coordinator,\n            config,\n            running_jobs: Arc::new(tokio::sync::RwLock::new(Vec::new())),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Start the worker loop.\n    ///\n    /// This runs continuously, polling for jobs and processing them.\n    pub async fn run(&self) -> Result<()> {\n        info!(\"Starting Mode C worker loop\");\n\n        let mut poll_interval = interval(Duration::from_millis(self.config.poll_interval_ms));\n        let mut heartbeat_interval = interval(Duration::from_millis(self.config.heartbeat_interval_ms));\n\n        loop {\n            tokio::select! {\n                _ = poll_interval.tick() => {\n                    if let Err(e) = self.poll_and_claim().await {\n                        error!(\"Error polling for jobs: {}\", e);\n                    }\n                }\n                _ = heartbeat_interval.tick() => {\n                    if let Err(e) = self.renew_claims().await {\n                        error!(\"Error renewing claims: {}\", e);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Poll for queued jobs and claim one if available.\n    async fn poll_and_claim(&self) -> Result<()> {\n        // Check if we're at capacity\n        let running = self.running_jobs.read().await;\n        if running.len() >= self.config.max_concurrent_jobs {\n            debug!(\"At capacity ({} jobs), skipping poll\", running.len());\n            return Ok(());\n        }\n        drop(running);\n\n        // Reclaim expired claims first\n        let reclaimed = self.coordinator.reclaim_expired_claims()?;\n        if reclaimed > 0 {\n            info!(\"Reclaimed {} expired job claims\", reclaimed);\n        }\n\n        // Try to claim a job\n        let claimed = match self.coordinator.claim_job()? {\n            Some(job) => job,\n            None => return Ok(()), // No jobs available\n        };\n\n        let job_id = claimed.id.clone();\n        let job_type_str = claimed.type_.clone();\n\n        info!(\"Claimed job {} (type: {})\", job_id, job_type_str);\n\n        // Parse job type and parameters\n        let job_type = JobType::from_str(&claimed.type_)\n            .ok_or_else(|| MiroirError::InvalidRequest(format!(\"unknown job type: {}\", claimed.type_)))?;\n        let params = claimed.parse_params()?;\n\n        // Check if this is a large job that needs chunking\n        if claimed.parent_job_id.is_none() && self.should_chunk(&job_type, &params) {\n            // Split into chunks and re-enqueue\n            self.split_and_enqueue(&claimed, &job_type, &params).await?;\n            return Ok(());\n        }\n\n        // Spawn a task to process the job\n        let running_job = RunningJob {\n            id: job_id.clone(),\n            type_: job_type,\n            params: params.clone(),\n            last_heartbeat: crate::mode_c_coordinator::now_ms(),\n        };\n\n        {\n            let mut running = self.running_jobs.write().await;\n            running.push(running_job);\n        }\n\n        let coordinator = self.coordinator.clone();\n        let running_jobs = self.running_jobs.clone();\n        let job_id_clone = job_id.clone();\n\n        tokio::spawn(async move {\n            let result = match job_type {\n                JobType::DumpImport => Self::process_dump_import(&coordinator, &job_id_clone, &params).await,\n                JobType::ReshardBackfill => Self::process_reshard_backfill(&coordinator, &job_id_clone, &params).await,\n            };\n\n            // Remove from running jobs\n            {\n                let mut running = running_jobs.write().await;\n                running.retain(|j| j.id != job_id_clone);\n            }\n\n            if let Err(e) = result {\n                error!(\"Job {} failed: {}\", job_id_clone, e);\n                let progress = JobProgress::default();\n                let _ = coordinator.fail_job(&job_id_clone, &progress, e.to_string());\n            }\n        });\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Renew claims for all running jobs.\n    async fn renew_claims(&self) -> Result<()> {\n        let running = self.running_jobs.read().await;\n        let now = crate::mode_c_coordinator::now_ms();\n\n        for job in running.iter() {\n            match self.coordinator.renew_claim(&job.id) {\n                Ok(true) => {\n                    debug!(\"Renewed claim for job {}\", job.id);\n                }\n                Ok(false) => {\n                    warn!(\"Failed to renew claim for job {} - may have lost ownership\", job.id);\n                }\n                Err(e) => {\n                    error!(\"Error renewing claim for job {}: {}\", job.id, e);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Check if a job should be split into chunks.\n    fn should_chunk(&self, job_type: &JobType, params: &JobParams) -> bool {\n        const DEFAULT_CHUNK_SIZE_BYTES: u64 = 268_435_456; // 256 MiB\n\n        match job_type {\n            JobType::DumpImport => {\n                // Chunk if source size exceeds 2x the default chunk size\n                if let Some(size) = params.source_size_bytes {\n                    size > DEFAULT_CHUNK_SIZE_BYTES * 2\n                } else {\n                    false\n                }\n            }\n            JobType::ReshardBackfill => {\n                // Chunk if old_shards exceeds 32 (configurable threshold)\n                if let Some(old_shards) = params.old_shards {\n                    old_shards > 32\n                } else {\n                    false\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Split a large job into chunks and enqueue them.\n    async fn split_and_enqueue(\n        &self,\n        claimed: &ClaimedJob,\n        job_type: &JobType,\n        params: &JobParams,\n    ) -> Result<()> {\n        let chunk_size_bytes = self.coordinator.default_chunk_size_bytes();\n\n        let chunks = match job_type {\n            JobType::DumpImport => {\n                // For dump import, split on byte offset boundaries\n                // In a full implementation, we would:\n                // 1. Fetch the dump data from params.source_url\n                // 2. Use dump_chunking::split_dump_into_chunks to split on NDJSON line boundaries\n                // For now, we create size-based chunks that will be aligned to line boundaries\n                // during actual processing by the worker that processes each chunk\n                let source_size = params.source_size_bytes.unwrap_or(0);\n                if source_size == 0 {\n                    return Err(MiroirError::InvalidRequest(\"source_size_bytes is required for dump import chunking\".into()));\n                }\n\n                // Calculate number of chunks (ceiling division)\n                let total_chunks = ((source_size + chunk_size_bytes - 1) / chunk_size_bytes) as u32;\n\n                (0..total_chunks)\n                    .map(|i| {\n                        let i = i as u64;\n                        let start = i * chunk_size_bytes;\n                        let end = std::cmp::min(start + chunk_size_bytes, source_size);\n                        JobChunk {\n                            index: i as u32,\n                            total: total_chunks,\n                            start: start.to_string(),\n                            end: end.to_string(),\n                            size_bytes: end - start,\n                        }\n                    })\n                    .collect()\n            }\n            JobType::ReshardBackfill => {\n                // Use reshard_chunking to split by shard-id range\n                let old_shards = params.old_shards.unwrap_or(1);\n                let target_shards = params.target_shards.unwrap_or(old_shards * 2);\n                let shards_per_chunk = 32; // Configurable shard count per chunk\n\n                let specs = reshard_chunking::split_reshard_into_chunks(\n                    old_shards,\n                    target_shards,\n                    shards_per_chunk,\n                );\n                reshard_chunking::reshard_specs_to_job_chunks(specs)\n            }\n        };\n\n        info!(\"Splitting job {} into {} chunks\", claimed.id, chunks.len());\n        self.coordinator.split_job_into_chunks(claimed, chunks)?;\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Process a dump import job.\n    async fn process_dump_import(\n        coordinator: &ModeCCoordinator,\n        job_id: &str,\n        params: &JobParams,\n    ) -> Result<()> {\n        info!(\"Processing dump import job {}\", job_id);\n\n        // If this is a chunk job, process the chunk\n        if let Some(chunk) = &params.chunk {\n            info!(\n                \"Processing dump chunk {}/{} (offsets {}-{})\",\n                chunk.index,\n                chunk.total,\n                chunk.start,\n                chunk.end\n            );\n\n            // Parse chunk boundaries\n            let          .map_err(|_| MiroirError::InvalidRequest(\"invalid chunk end offset\".into()))?;\n\n            // Process the dump import chunk\n            let result = Self::process_dump_chunk(\n                coordinator,\n                job_id,\n                params,\n                start_offset,\n                end_offset,\n            ).await;\n\n            match result {\n                Ok((bytes_processed, docs_routed, last_cursor)) => {\n                    let progress = JobProgress {\n                        bytes_processed,\n                        docs_routed,\n                        last_cursor,\n                        error: None,\n                    };\n                    coordinator.complete_job(job_id, &progress)?;\n                    info!(\n                        \"Completed dump chunk {}/{}: {} bytes, {} docs\",\n                        chunk.index, chunk.total, bytes_processed, docs_routed\n                    );\n                }\n                Err(e) => {\n                    let progress = JobProgress {\n                        bytes_processed: start_offset,\n                        docs_routed: 0,\n                        last_cursor: start_offset.to_string(),\n                        error: Some(e.to_string()),\n                    };\n                    coordinator.fail_job(job_id, &progress, e.to_string())?;\n                    return Err(e);\n                }\n            }\n        } else {\n            // Parent job was already split, mark as delegated\n            let progress = JobProgress {\n                bytes_processed: 0,\n                docs_routed: 0,\n                last_cursor: \"delegated\".to_string(),\n                error: None,\n            };\n\n            coordinator.complete_job(job_id, &progress)?;\n        }\n\n        info!(\"Completed dump import job {}\", job_id);\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Process a single dump chunk.\n    ///\n    /// This is a simulation of the full dump import processing. In production,\n    /// this would:\n    /// 1. Fetch dump data from params.source_url with Range header\n    /// 2. Parse NDJSON lines (align to line boundaries)\n    /// 3. Route each document to target shard based on primary_key\n    /// 4. Update progress periodically (heartbeat)\n    /// 5. Handle idempotent resume from last_cursor\n    async fn process_dump_chunk(\n        coordinator: &ModeCCoordinator,\n        job_id: &str,\n        params: &JobParams,\n        start_offset: u64,\n        end_offset: u64,\n    ) -> Result<(u64, u64, String)> {\n        use crate::router::shard_for_key;\n        use std::time::{Duration, Instant};\n\n        let chunk_size = end_offset - start_offset;\n        let shard_count = params.shard_count.unwrap_or(64);\n        let primary_key = params.primary_key.as_deref().unwrap_or(\"id\");\n\n        // Simulate processing in batches to allow for progress updates\n        let batch_size = 10_000_000; // 10 MB batches\n        let mut bytes_processed = 0u64;\n        let mut docs_routed = 0u64;\n        let mut last_cursor = start_offset.to_string();\n\n        let start_time = Instant::now();\n        let heartbeat_interval = Duration::from_secs(5);\n\n        while bytes_processed < chunk_size {\n            let batch_end = std::cmp::min(bytes_processed + batch_size, chunk_size);\n            let batch_bytes = batch_end - bytes_processed;\n\n            // Simulate processing time based on batch size\n            // In production, this would be actual I/O and processing\n            let simulate_delay = Duration::from_millis((batch_bytes / 1_000_000) * 10);\n            tokio::time::sleep(simulate_delay).await;\n\n            // Simulate document routing\n            // Estimate ~100KB per document (typical JSON document)\n            let estimated_docs = batch_bytes / 100_000;\n            for i in 0..estimated_docs {\n                // Simulate document key\n                let doc_key = format!(\"{}-{}-{}\", primary_key, start_offset + bytes_processed, i);\n                let _shard_id = shard_for_key(&doc_key, shard_count);\n                // In production, we would route the document to the target node/shard\n            }\n\n            bytes_processed = batch_end;\n            docs_routed += estimated_docs;\n            last_cursor = (start_offset + bytes_processed).to_string();\n\n            // Update progress periodically\n            let elapsed = start_time.elapsed();\n            if elapsed >= heartbeat_interval {\n                // Update progress and renew claim\n                let progress = JobProgress {\n                    bytes_processed,\n                    docs_routed,\n                    last_cursor: last_cursor.clone(),\n                    error: None,\n                };\n                coordinator.update_progress(job_id, &progress, crate::mode_c_coordinator::JobState::InProgress)?;\n\n                // Renew the claim\n                let _ = coordinator.renew_claim(job_id);\n\n                // Reset the timer\n                let _ = start_time.elapsed();\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok((bytes_processed, docs_routed, last_cursor))\n    }\n\n    /// Process a reshard backfill job.\n    async fn process_reshard_backfill(\n        coordinator: &ModeCCoordinator,\n        job_id: &str,\n        params: &JobParams,\n    ) -> Result<()> {\n        info!(\"Processing reshard backfill job {}\", job_id);\n\n        // If this is a chunk job, process the shard range\n        if let Some(chunk) = &params.chunk {\n            let (start_shard, end_shard) = reshard backfill chunk\n            let result = Self::process_reshard_chunk(\n                coordinator,\n                job_id,\n                params,\n                start_shard,\n                end_shard,\n            ).await;\n\n            match result {\n                Ok((docs_backfilled, last_cursor)) => {\n                    let progress = JobProgress {\n                        bytes_processed: 0, // Not applicable for reshard\n                        docs_routed: docs_backfilled,\n                        last_cursor,\n                        error: None,\n                    };\n                    coordinator.complete_job(job_id, &progress)?;\n                    info!(\n                        \"Completed reshard chunk {}/{}: {} docs from shards {}-{}\",\n                        chunk.index, chunk.total, docs_backfilled, start_shard, end_shard\n                    );\n                }\n                Err(e) => {\n                    let progress = JobProgress {\n                        bytes_processed: 0,\n                        docs_routed: 0,\n                        last_cursor: start_shard.to_string(),\n                        error: Some(e.to_string()),\n                    };\n                    coordinator.fail_job(job_id, &progress, e.to_string())?;\n                    return Err(e);\n                }\n            }\n        } else {\n            // Parent job was already split, mark as delegated\n            let progress = JobProgress {\n                bytes_processed: 0,\n                docs_routed: 0,\n                last_cursor: \"delegated\".to_string(),\n                error: None,\n            };\n\n            coordinator.complete_job(job_id, &progress)?;\n        }\n\n        info!(\"Completed reshard backfill job {}\", job_id);\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Process a single reshard backfill chunk.\n    ///\n    /// This is a simulation of the full reshard backfill processing. In production,\n    /// this would:\n    /// 1. Read documents from old shard range [start_shard, end_shard)\n    /// 2. Re-route each document to new shard configuration\n    /// 3. Update progress periodically (heartbeat)\n    /// 4. Handle idempotent resume from last_cursor\n    async fn process_reshard_chunk(\n        coordinator: &ModeCCoordinator,\n        job_id: &str,\n        params: &JobParams,\n        start_shard: u32,\n        end_shard: u32,\n    ) -> Result<(u64, String)> {\n        use crate::router::{shard_for_key, assign_shard_in_group};\n        use crate::topology::{Topology, Group, NodeId};\n        use std::time::{Duration, Instant};\n\n        let old_shards = params.old_shards.unwrap_or(64);\n        let target_shards = params.target_shards.unwrap_or(128);\n        let shard_count = (end_shard - start_shard) as u64;\n\n        // Simulate processing in batches to allow for progress updates\n        let batch_shards = 4; // Process 4 shards at a time\n        let mut shards_processed = 0u32;\n        let mut docs_backfilled = 0u64;\n        let mut last_cursor = start_shard.to_string();\n\n        let start_time = Instant::now();\n        let heartbeat_interval = Duration::from_secs(5);\n\n        // Create a simple topology for routing simulation\n        let topology = Topology::new(2, 1, 3); // 2 groups, 1 RF, 3 nodes per group\n\n        while start_shard + shards_processed < end_shard {\n            let batch_end = std::cmp::min(start_shard + shards_processed + batch_shards, end_shard);\n            let batch_count = (batch_end - (start_shard + shards_processed)) as u64;\n\n            // Simulate document processing for each shard\n            // Estimate ~1000 documents per shard\n            for shard_id in (start_shard + shards_processed)..batch_end {\n                let estimated_docs = 1000u64;\n\n                for i in 0..estimated_docs {\n                    // Simulate document key\n                    let doc_key = format!(\"doc-shard{}-{}\", shard_id, i);\n\n                    // Compute old shard assignment\n                    let _old_shard = shard_for_key(&doc_key, old_shards);\n\n                    // Compute new shard assignment\n                    let new_shard = shard_for_key(&doc_key, target_shards);\n\n                    // In production, we would:\n                    // 1. Read the document from the old shard\n                    // 2. Write it to the new shard assignment\n                    // 3. Handle any conflicts or duplicates\n\n                    // Simulate routing to replica groups\n                    for group in topology.groups() {\n                        let _targets = assign_shard_in_group(new_shard, group.nodes(), topology.rf());\n                        // In production, we would write to these target nodes\n                    }\n                }\n\n                docs_backfilled += estimated_docs;\n            }\n\n            shards_processed = batch_end - start_shard;\n            last_cursor = (start_shard + shards_processed as u32).to_string();\n\n            // Update progress periodically\n            let elapsed = start_time.elapsed();\n            if elapsed >= heartbeat_interval {\n                // Update progress and renew claim\n                let progress = JobProgress {\n                    bytes_processed: 0,\n                    docs_routed: docs_backfilled,\n                    last_cursor: last_cursor.clone(),\n                    error: None,\n                };\n                coordinator.update_progress(job_id, &progress, crate::mode_c_coordinator::JobState::InProgress)?;\n\n                // Renew the claim\n                let _ = coordinator.renew_claim(job_id);\n\n                // Reset the timer\n                let _ = start_time.elapsed();\n            }\n\n            // Simulate processing time\n            tokio::time::sleep(Duration::from_millis(50)).await;\n        }\n\n        Ok((docs_backfilled, last_cursor))\n    }\n}\n","numLines":613,"startLine":1,"totalLines":613}}}

Mode C work-queued chunked jobs coordinator (plan §14.5 Mode C).\n//!\n//! Any pod can claim a queued job via compare-and-swap. Jobs have claim TTL\n//! with heartbeats; expired claims are released for reclamation.\n//!\n//! Large jobs are split into chunks on input boundaries by the first pod\n//! that picks them up. Each chunk is an independent job with a parent reference.\n//!\n//! Applied to:\n//! - §13.9 streaming dump import — chunks on NDJSON line boundaries\n//! - §13.1 reshard backfill — partitions by shard-id range\n//!\n//! ## HPA Queue Depth Metric (plan §14.4)\n//!\n//! The coordinator provides a queue depth metric for Horizontal Pod Autoscaler:\n//!\n//! ```text\n//! miroir:jobs:_queued (Redis set)\n//! SCARD miroir:jobs:_queued = miroir_background_queue_depth\n//! ```\n//!\n//! The HPA can be configured to scale on this external metric:\n//!\n//! ```yaml\n//! metrics:\n//! - type: External\n//!   external:\n//!     metric:\n//!       name: miroir_background_queue_depth\n//!     target:\n//!       type: AverageValue\n//!       averageValue: 10\n//! ```\n//!\n//! Example HPA configuration that scales up when queue depth > 10:\n//! ```yaml\n//! apiVersion: autoscaling/v2\n//! kind: HorizontalPodAutoscaler\n//! metadata:\n//!   name: miroir-worker-hpa\n//! spec:\n//!   scaleTargetRef:\n//!     apiVersion: apps/v1\n//!     kind: Deployment\n//!     name: miroir-worker\n//!   minReplicas: 2\n//!   maxReplicas: 10\n//!   metrics:\n//!   - type: External\n//!     external:\n//!       metric:\n//!         name: miroir_background_queue_depth\n//!       target:\n//!         type: AverageValue\n//!         averageValue: 10\n//! ```\n\nuse crate::error::{MiroirError, Result};\nuse crate::task_store::{JobRow, NewJob, TaskStore};\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\nuse std::sync::Arc;\nuse std::time::{SystemTime, UNIX_EPOCH};\nuse tracing::{debug, info, warn, error};\n\n/// Job states (plan §14.5 Mode C).\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n#[repr(u8)]\npub enum JobState {\n    /// Job is queued and waiting to be claimed.\n    Queued = 0,\n    /// Job is claimed and in progress.\n    InProgress = 1,\n    /// Job completed successfully.\n    Completed = 2,\n    /// Job failed.\n    Failed = 3,\n}\n\nimpl JobState {\n    /// Parse from string.\n    pub fn from_str(s: &str) -> Option<Self> {\n        match s {\n            \"queued\" => Some(Self::Queued),\n            \"in_progress\" => Some(Self::InProgress),\n            \"completed\" => Some(Self::Completed),\n            \"failed\" => Some(Self::Failed),\n            _ => None,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Convert to string.\n    pub fn as_str(&self) -> &'static str {\n        match self {\n            Self::Queued => \"queued\",\n            Self::InProgress => \"in_progress\",\n            Self::Completed => \"completed\",\n            Self::Failed => \"failed\",\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Job types supported by Mode C coordinator.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum JobType {\n    /// Streaming dump import (plan §13.9).\n    DumpImport = 0,\n    /// Reshard backfill (plan §13.1).\n    ReshardBackfill = 1,\n}\n\nimpl JobType {\n    /// Parse from string.\n    pub fn from_str(s: &str) -> Option<Self> {\n        match s {\n            \"dump_import\" => Some(Self::DumpImport),\n            \"reshard_backfill\" => Some(Self::ReshardBackfill),\n            _ => None,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Convert to string.\n    pub fn as_str(&self) -> &'static str {\n        match self {\n            Self::DumpImport => \"dump_import\",\n            Self::ReshardBackfill => \"reshard_backfill\",\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Job progress tracking.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct JobProgress {\n    /// Bytes processed so far (for dump import).\n    pub bytes_processed: u64,\n    /// Documents routed so far (for dump import).\n    pub docs_routed: u64,\n    /// Last cursor position for idempotent resume.\n    pub last_cursor: String,\n    /// Any error message.\n    pub error: Option<String>,\n}\n\nimpl Default for JobProgress {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            bytes_processed: 0,\n            docs_routed: 0,\n            last_cursor: String::new(),\n            error: None,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Chunk specification for a job.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct JobChunk {\n    /// Chunk index (0-based).\n    pub index: u32,\n    /// Total number of chunks.\n    pub total: u32,\n    /// Starting position (cursor or byte offset).\n    pub start: String,\n    /// Ending position (cursor or byte offset).\n    pub end: String,\n    /// Estimated size in bytes.\n    pub size_bytes: u64,\n}\n\n/// Job parameters.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct JobParams {\n    /// Index UID being operated on.\n    pub index_uid: String,\n    /// Primary key field (for dump import).\n    pub primary_key: Option<String>,\n    /// Shard count (for dump import routing).\n    pub shard_count: Option<u32>,\n    /// Old shard count (for reshard backfill).\n    pub old_shards: Option<u32>,\n    /// Target shard count (for reshard backfill).\n    pub target_shards: Option<u32>,\n    /// Shadow index UID (for reshard backfill).\n    pub shadow_index: Option<String>,\n    /// Chunk specification (if this is a chunk).\n    pub chunk: Option<JobChunk>,\n    /// Source data location (for dump import).\n    pub source_url: Option<String>,\n    /// Source data size (for dump import).\n    pub source_size_bytes: Option<u64>,\n}\n\n/// Mode C job coordinator.\n#[derive(Clone)]\npub struct ModeCCoordinator {\n    /// Task store for job persistence.\n    task_store: Arc<dyn TaskStore>,\n    /// Pod ID for claiming jobs.\n    pod_id: String,\n    /// Claim TTL in milliseconds (default 30s).\n    claim_ttl_ms: i64,\n    /// Heartbeat interval in milliseconds (default 10s).\n    heartbeat_interval_ms: i64,\n    /// Default chunk size in bytes (default 256 MiB).\n    default_chunk_size_bytes: u64,\n}\n\nimpl ModeCCoordinator {\n    /// Create a new Mode C coordinator.\n    pub fn new(\n        task_store: Arc<dyn TaskStore>,\n        pod_id: String,\n    ) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            task_store,\n            pod_id,\n            claim_ttl_ms: 30_000,  // 30 seconds\n            heartbeat_interval_ms: 10_000,  // 10 seconds\n            default_chunk_size_bytes: 268_435_456,  // 256 MiB\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Set the claim TTL.\n    pub fn with_claim_ttl_ms(mut self, ttl_ms: i64) -> Self {\n        self.claim_ttl_ms = ttl_ms;\n        self\n    }\n\n    /// Set the heartbeat interval.\n    pub fn with_heartbeat_interval_ms(mut self, interval_ms: i64) -> Self {\n        self.heartbeat_interval_ms = interval_ms;\n        self\n    }\n\n    /// Set the default chunk size.\n    pub fn with_chunk_size_bytes(mut self, size_bytes: u64) -> Self {\n        self.default_chunk_size_bytes = size_bytes;\n        self\n    }\n\n    /// Get the default chunk size in bytes.\n    pub fn default_chunk_size_bytes(&self) -> u64 {\n        self.default_chunk_size_bytes\n    }\n\n    /// Enqueue a new job.\n    pub fn enqueue_job(\n        &self,\n        type_: JobType,\n        params: JobParams,\n    ) -> Result<String> {\n        let job_id = format!(\"{}-{}\", type_.as_str(), uuid::Uuid::new_v4());\n        let params_json = serde_json::to_string(&params)\n            .map_err(|e| MiroirError::TaskStore(format!(\"failed to serialize params: {}\", e)))?;\n        let progress = JobProgress::default();\n        let progress_json = serde_json::to_string(&progress)\n            .map_err(|e| MiroirError::TaskStore(format!(\"failed to serialize progress: {}\", e)))?;\n\n        let new_job = NewJob {\n            id: job_id.clone(),\n            type_: type_.as_str().to_string(),\n            params: params_json,\n            state: JobState::Queued.as_str().to_string(),\n            progress: progress_json,\n            parent_job_id: None,\n            chunk_index: None,\n            total_chunks: None,\n            created_at: now_ms(),\n        };\n\n        self.task_store.insert_job(&new_job)?;\n\n        debug!(\n            job_id = %job_id,\n            job_type = %type_.as_str(),\n            \"enqueued new Mode C job\"\n        );\n\n        Ok(job_id)\n    }\n\n    /// Try to claim a queued job.\n    ///\n    /// Returns the claimed job if successful, or None if no jobs are available.\n    pub fn claim_job(&self) -> Result<Option<ClaimedJob>> {\n        // List queued jobs\n        let queued_jobs = self.task_store.list_jobs_by_state(JobState::Queued.as_str())?;\n\n        if queued_jobs.is_empty() {\n            return Ok(None);\n        }\n\n        // Try to claim the first available job\n        let now = now_ms();\n        let claim_expires_at = now + self.claim_ttl_ms;\n\n        for job in queued_jobs {\n            if self.task_store.claim_job(&job.id, &self.pod_id, claim_expires_at)? {\n                // Successfully claimed\n                debug!(\n                    job_id = %job.id,\n                    pod_id = %self.pod_id,\n                    \"claimed Mode C job\"\n                );\n\n                return Ok(Some(ClaimedJob {\n                    id: job.id.clone(),\n                    type_: job.type_.clone(),\n                    params: job.params.clone(),\n                    progress: job.progress.clone(),\n                    claimed_by: self.pod_id.clone(),\n                    claim_expires_at,\n                    parent_job_id: job.parent_job_id.clone(),\n                    chunk_index: job.chunk_index,\n                    total_chunks: job.total_chunks,\n                }));\n            }\n        }\n\n        // All queued jobs were claimed by another pod\n        Ok(None)\n    }\n\n    /// Renew a job claim (heartbeat).\n    ///\n    /// Returns true if the claim was renewed, false if we lost the claim.\n    pub fn renew_claim(&self, job_id: &str) -> Result<bool> {\n        let now = now_ms();\n        let claim_expires_at = now + self.claim_ttl_ms;\n\n        let renewed = self.task_store.renew_job_claim(job_id, claim_expires_at)?;\n\n        if !renewed {\n            warn!(\n                job_id = %job_id,\n                pod_id = %self.pod_id,\n                \"failed to renew job claim - may have lost ownership\"\n            );\n        }\n\n        Ok(renewed)\n    }\n\n    /// Update job progress.\n    pub fn update_progress(\n        &self,\n        job_id: &str,\n        progress: &JobProgress,\n        state: JobState,\n    ) -> Result<()> {\n        let progress_json = serde_json::to_string(progress)\n            .map_err(|e| MiroirError::TaskStore(format!(\"failed to serialize progress: {}\", e)))?;\n\n        self.task_store.update_job_progress(job_id, state.as_str(), &progress_json)?;\n\n        debug!(\n            job_id = %job_id,\n            state = %state.as_str(),\n            bytes_processed = progress.bytes_processed,\n            \"updated job progress\"\n        );\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Complete a job successfully.\n    pub fn complete_job(&self, job_id: &str, progress: &JobProgress) -> Result<()> {\n        self.update_progress(job_id, progress, JobState::Completed)?;\n\n        info!(\n            job_id = %job_id,\n            \"completed Mode C job\"\n        );\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Fail a job.\n    pub fn fail_job(&self, job_id: &str, progress: &JobProgress, error: String) -> Result<()> {\n        let mut failed_progress = progress.clone();\n        failed_progress.error = Some(error.clone());\n\n        let progress_json = serde_json::to_string(&failed_progress)\n            .map_err(|e| MiroirError::TaskStore(format!(\"failed to serialize progress: {}\", e)))?;\n\n        self.task_store.update_job_progress(job_id, JobState::Failed.as_str(), &progress_json)?;\n\n        error!(\n            job_id = %job_id,\n            error = %error,\n            \"failed Mode C job\"\n        );\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Split a large job into chunks and enqueue them.\n    ///\n    /// Called by the first pod that picks up a large job. The original job\n    /// transitions to \"delegated\" state and child chunk jobs are created.\n    pub fn split_job_into_chunks(\n        &self,\n        job: &ClaimedJob,\n        chunk_specs: Vec<JobChunk>,\n    ) -> Result<Vec<String>> {\n        let params: JobParams = serde_json::from_str(&job.params)\n            .map_err(|e| MiroirError::TaskStore(format!(\"failed to deserialize params: {}\", e)))?;\n\n        let total_chunks = chunk_specs.len() as u32;\n        let mut chunk_job_ids = Vec::new();\n\n        // Mark the parent job as delegated (in_progress with special progress)\n        let delegated_progress = JobProgress {\n            bytes_processed: 0,\n            docs_routed: 0,\n            last_cursor: \"delegated\".to_string(),\n            error: None,\n        };\n        self.update_progress(&job.id, &delegated_progress, JobState::InProgress)?;\n\n        // Create chunk jobs\n        for (idx, chunk) in chunk_specs.iter().enumerate() {\n            let mut chunk_params = params.clone();\n            chunk_params.chunk = Some(chunk.clone());\n\n            let chunk_job_id = format!(\"{}-chunk-{}\", job.id, idx);\n            let params_json = serde_json::to_string(&chunk_params)\n                .map_err(|e| MiroirError::TaskStore(format!(\"failed to serialize chunk params: {}\", e)))?;\n            let progress = JobProgress::default();\n            let progress_json = serde_json::to_string(&progress)\n                .map_err(|e| MiroirError::TaskStore(format!(\"failed to serialize progress: {}\", e)))?;\n\n            let new_job = NewJob {\n                id: chunk_job_id.clone(),\n                type_: job.type_.clone(),\n                params: params_json,\n                state: JobState::Queued.as_str().to_string(),\n                progress: progress_json,\n                parent_job_id: Some(job.id.clone()),\n                chunk_index: Some(idx as i64),\n                total_chunks: Some(total_chunks as i64),\n                created_at: now_ms(),\n            };\n\n            self.task_store.insert_job(&new_job)?;\n            chunk_job_ids.push(chunk_job_id);\n        }\n\n        info!(\n            parent_job_id = %job.id,\n            chunk_count = total_chunks,\n            \"split job into chunks\"\n        );\n\n        Ok(chunk_job_ids)\n    }\n\n    /// Reclaim expired claims.\n    ///\n    /// Returns the number of claims reclaimed.\n    /// Preserves job progress for idempotent resume.\n    pub fn reclaim_expired_claims(&self) -> Result<usize> {\n        let now = now_ms();\n        let expired_jobs = self.task_store.list_expired_claims(now)?;\n\n        let mut reclaimed = 0;\n        for job in expired_jobs {\n            // Preserve the existing progress for idempotent resume\n            // The job.progress field contains the last_cursor and other state\n            // needed by the next pod to resume from where the previous pod left off\n            let progress_json = job.progress.clone();\n\n            // Clear claim and reset to queued\n            self.task_store.reclaim_job_claim(&job.id, JobState::Queued.as_str(), &progress_json)?;\n\n            debug!(\n                job_id = %job.id,\n                previous_claimant = ?job.claimed_by,\n                \"reclaimed expired job claim\"\n            );\n\n            reclaimed += 1;\n        }\n\n        if reclaimed > 0 {\n            info!(\n                count = reclaimed,\n                \"reclaimed expired job claims\"\n            );\n        }\n\n        Ok(reclaimed)\n    }\n\n    /// Get the queue depth (number of queued jobs).\n    ///\n    /// Used for HPA scaling per plan §14.4.\n    pub fn queue_depth(&self) -> Result<u64> {\n        self.task_store.count_jobs_by_state(JobState::Queued.as_str())\n    }\n\n    /// Get job by ID.\n    pub fn get_job(&self, job_id: &str) -> Result<Option<JobRow>> {\n        self.task_store.get_job(job_id)\n    }\n\n    /// List all chunks for a parent job.\n    pub fn list_chunks(&self, parent_job_id: &str) -> Result<Vec<JobRow>> {\n        self.task_store.list_jobs_by_parent(parent_job_id)\n    }\n\n    /// List jobs by state.\n    pub fn list_jobs_by_state(&self, state: &str) -> Result<Vec<JobRow>> {\n        self.task_store.list_jobs_by_state(state)\n    }\n\n    /// Set the claim expiration time for a job (test helper).\n    ///\n    /// This allows tests to simulate time passing without actually self.task_store.renew_job_claim(job_id, expires_at)?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n/// A claimed job being processed by a pod.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct ClaimedJob {\n    /// Job ID.\n self.parent_job_id.is_some()\n    }\n\n    /// Check if the claim is about to expire (within 5 seconds).\n    pub fn claim_expiring_soon(&self) -> bool {\n        let now = now_ms();\n        self.claim_expires_at - now < 5_000\n    }\n}\n\n/// Get current UNIX timestamp in milliseconds.\npub fn now_ms() -> i64 {\n    SystemTime::now()\n        .duration_since(UNIX_EPOCH)\n test_acceptance_claim_expires_after_30s() {\n    // Acceptance: Kill a claimant mid-chunk: claim expires in 30s;\n    // another pod picks up and resumes at last_cursor\n    let store = Arc::new(SqliteTaskStore::open_in_memory().unwrap());\n    store.migrate().unwrap();\n\n    let coord1 = test_coordinator_with_store(\"pod-1\", store.clone());\n\n    // Enqueue a job\n    let params test_acceptance_three_pods_claim_chunks_in_parallel() {\n    // Acceptance: 3 pods claim 3 of 4 chunks in parallel; queue drains\n    // Tests that multiple pods can claim chunks from the same parent job\n    let store = Arc::new(SqliteTaskStore::open_in_memory().unwrap());\n    store.migrate().unwrap();\n\n    // Enqueue a 1GB dump import job\n    let params = dump_import_params(1_073_741_824); // 1 GiB\n    let job_id = {\n        let coord = test_coordinator_with_store(\"pod-1\", store.clone());\n        coord.enqueue_job(JobType::DumpImport, params).unwrap()\n    };\n\n    // Pod 1 claims the job and splits it into 4 chunks\n    let coord1 = test_coordinator_with_store(\"pod-1\", store.clone());\n    let claimed = coord1.claim_job().unwrap().expect(\"pod-1 should claim job\");\n assert_eq!(child_jobs.len(), 4);\n    assert_eq!(coord1.queue_depth().unwrap(), 4);\n\n    // Create 3 coordinators representing 3 different pods\n    let coord2 = test_coordinator_with_store(\"pod-2\", store.clone());\n    let coord3 = test_coordinator_with_store(\"pod-3\", store.clone());\n\n    // Pod 1 claims a chunk\n    let claimed1 = coord1.claim_job().unwrap().expect(\"pod-1 should claim a chunk\");\n    assert!(claimed1.parent_job_id.is_some()); // It's a chunk job\n    assert_eq!(coord1.queue_depth().unwrap(), 3);\n\n    // Pod Different chunks\n    assert_eq!(coord2.queue_depth().unwrap(), 2);\n\n    // Pod 3 claims a chunk\n    let claimed3 = coord3.claim_job().unwrap().expect(\"pod-3 should claim a chunk\");\n assert_eq!(coord3.queue_depth().unwrap(), 1);\n\n    // 1 chunk remains queued\n    assert_eq!(coord1.queue_depth().unwrap(), 1);\n\n    // Pods complete their chunks\n    let progress = JobProgress::default();\n    coord1.complete_job(&claimed1.id, &progress).unwrap();\n    coord2.complete_job(&claimed2.id, &progress).unwrap();\n    coord3.complete_job(&claimed3.id, &progress).unwrap();\n\n    // Queue depth should be 1 (remaining chunk)\n    assert_eq!(coord1.queue_depth().unwrap(), 1);\n\n    // Pod 1 claims and completes the final chunk\n    let claimed4 = coord1.claim_job().unwrap().expect(\"pod-1 should claim final chunk\");\n    coord1.complete_job(&claimed4.id, &progress).unwrap();\n\n    // Queue is now drained\n    assert_eq!(coord1.queue_depth().unwrap(), 0);\n}\n\n#[test]\nfn test_acceptance_reshard_backfill_chunking() {\n    // Acceptance: Reshard backfill with 64 old shards splits into chunks\n    let coord {\n772\t    let coordinator = test_coordinator(\"pod-1\");\n773\t\n774\t    // Enqueue and claim a job\n775\t    let params = JobParams {\n776\t        index_uid: \"test-index\".to_string(),\n777\t        primary_key: Some(\"id\".to_string()),\n778\t        shard_count: Some(64),\n779\t        old_shards: None,\n780\t        target_shards: None,\n781\t        shadow_index: None,\n782\t        chunk: None,\n783\t        source_url: Some(\"https://example.com/dump.ndjson\".to_string()),\n784\t        source_size_bytes: Some(1_000_000_000),\n785\t    };\n786\t\n787\t    let job_id = coordinator\n788\t        .enqueue_job(JobType::DumpImport, params)\n789\t        .unwrap();\n790\t\n791\t    let claimed = coordinator.claim_job().unwrap().unwrap();\n792\t    let original_expires_at = claimed.claim_expires_at;\n793\t\n794\t    // Sleep a bit to ensure time advances\n795\t    sleep(Duration::from_millis(10)).await;\n796\t\n797\t    // Renew the claim (heartbeat)\n798\t    let coordinator.get_job(&job_id).unwrap().unwrap();\n803\t    assert!(job.claim_expires_at.unwrap() > original_expires_at);\n804\t\n805\t    // Simulate missed heartbeat by setting expiration to the 256 MiB chunks; 3 pods claim 3 of 4 chunks in parallel.\n#[tokio::test]\nasync fn p6_5_a1_one_gb_dump_splits_into_chunks_processed_in_parallel() {\n    let store = Arc::new(MockTaskStore::new());\n\n    let pod1_coordinator = test_coordinator_with_store(\"pod-1\", store.clone());\n    let pod2_coordinator = test_coordinator_with_store(\"pod-2\", store.clone());\n    let pod3_coordinator = Some(\"https://example.com/dump.ndjson\".to_string()),\n        source_size_bytes: Some(1_000_000_000), // 1 GB\n    };\n\n    let parent_job_id = pod1_coordinator\n   let total_chunks = ((1_000_000_000 + chunk_size_bytes - 1) / chunk_size_bytes) as u32;\n    assert_eq!(total_chunks, 4);\n\n    let chunks: Vec<JobChunk> = (0..total_chunks)\n        .map(|i| {\n            let i = i as u64;\n            let start = i * chunk_size_bytes;\n            let end = std::cmp::min(start + chunk_size_bytes, 1_000_000_000);\n            JobChunk {\n                index:        .collect();\n\n    pod1_coordinator\n        .split_job_into_chunks(&claimed, chunks)\n        .unwrap();\n\n    // Verify 4 chunk jobs were created\n    let child_jobs = pod1_coordinator.list_chunks(&parent_job_id).unwrap();\n    assert_eq!(child_jobs.len(), 4);\n\n    // Each chunk should be in queued state\n    for child in &child_jobs {\n        assert_eq!(child.state, \"queued\");\n        assert_eq!(child.parent_job_id, Some(parent_job_id.clone()));\n    }\n\n    // Simulate 3 pods claiming 3 of the 4 chunks in parallel\n    let pod2_claimed = pod2_coordinator.claim_job().unwrap().unwrap();\n    let pod3_claimed = pod3_coordinator.claim_job().unwrap().unwrap();\n    let pod1_claimed_chunk = pod1_coordinator.claim_job().unwrap().unwrap();\n\n    // Verify each pod claimed a different chunk\n    let claimed_ids = vec![\n        pod2_claimed.id.clone(),\n        pod3_claimed.id.clone(),\n        pod1_claimed_chunk.id.clone(),\n    ];\n    assert_eq!(claimed_ids.len(), 3); // 3 distinct claims\n\n    // Verify all claimed chunks are now in_progress\n    for job_id in &claimed_ids {\n        let job = pod1_coordinator.get_job(job_id).unwrap().unwrap();\n        assert_eq!(job.state, \"in_progress\");\n    }\n\n    // One chunk remains queued (unclaimed)\n    let queued_jobs = pod1_coordinator.list_jobs_by_state(\"queued\").unwrap();\n    assert_eq!(queued_jobs.len(), 1);\n\n    // Queue depth should be 1 (the remaining chunk)\n    let queue_depth = pod1_coordinator.queue_depth().unwrap();\n    assert_eq!(queue_depth, 1);\n}\n\n/// P6.5-A2: Kill a claimant mid-chunk; claim expires in 30s; another pod picks up and resumes at last_cursor.\n#[tokio::test]\nasync fn p6_5_a2_claim_expiration_allows_resume_at_last_cursor() {\n    let store = Arc::new(MockTaskStore::new());\n\n    let pod1_coordinator = test_coordinator_with_store(\"pod-1\", store.clone());\n    let pod2_coordinator = test_coordinator_with_store(\"pod-2\", store);\n\n    // Enqueue and claim a job\n    let params = JobParams {\n       .enqueue_job(JobType::DumpImport, params.clone())\n        .unwrap();\n\n    let claimed = pod1_coordinator.claim_job().unwrap().unwrap();\n    assert_eq!(claimed.claimed_by, \"pod-1\");\n\n `miroir_background_queue_depth > 10` triggers scale-up; scale-down once empty.\n#[tokio::test]\nasync fn p6_5_a3_queue_depth_metric_drives_hpa_scaling() {\n    let coordinator = test_coordinator(\"pod-1\");\n\n    // Initially, queue is empty\n    let queue_depth = coordinator.queue_depth().unwrap();\n    assert_eq!(queue_depth, 0);\n\n    // Enqueue 15 jobs (above HPA threshold of 10)\n    for i in 0..15 {\n        let params = JobParams {\n            index_uid: format!(\"test-index-{}\", i),\n            primary_key: Some(\"id\".to_string()),\n            shard_count: Some(64),\n            old_shards: None,\n            target_shards: None,\n            shadow_index: None,\n            chunk: None,\n            source_url: Some(format!(\"https://example.com/dump{}.ndjson\", i)),\n            source_size_bytes: Some(1_000_000_000),\n        };\n\n        coordinator\n            .enqueue_job(JobType::DumpImport, params)\n            .unwrap();\n    }\n\n    // Queue depth should be 15\n    let queue_depth = coordinator.queue_depth().unwrap();\n    assert_eq!(queue_depth, 15);\n\n    // HPA would scale up when queue_depth > 10\n    let should_scale_up = queue_depth > 10;\n    assert!(should_scale_up);\n\n    // Simulate processing: claim and complete jobs\n    for _ in 0..15 {\n        if let Some(claimed) = coordinator.claim_job().unwrap() {\n            let progress = JobProgress {\n                bytes_processed: 1_000_000_000,\n                docs_routed: 10_000_000,\n                last_cursor: \"1000000000\".to_string(),\n                error: None,\n            };\n\n            coordinator\n                .complete_job(&claimed.id, &progress)\n                .unwrap();\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Queue depth should now be 0\n    let queue_depth = coordinator.queue_depth().unwrap();\n    assert_eq!(queue_depth, 0);\n\n    // HPA would scale down when queue is empty\n    let should_scale_down = queue_depth == 0;\n    assert!(should_scale_down);\n}\n\n/// P6.5-A4: Two concurrent dumps; chunks interleave in claims; neither starves.\n#[tokio::test]\nasync fn p6_5_a4_concurrent_dumps_interleave_without_starvation() {\n    let store = Arc::new(MockTaskStore::new());\n\n    let pod1_coordinator = test_coordinator_with_store(\"pod-1\", store.clone());\n .enqueue_job(JobType::DumpImport, params1)\n        .unwrap();\n    let job_id2 = pod1_coordinator\n        .enqueue_job(JobType::DumpImport, params2)\n        .unwrap();\n\n    // Pod 1 claims first
